On the morning of the 31st, a Japanese athlete suddenly discovered that several dozen yen were missing from his clothes hanging on the wall. Because everyone was in the washroom at the time and the door was not locked, they suspected a servant and reported it to the police. Two criminal police officers went to investigate and determined that a certain Filipino boxer was highly suspected. He was brought to the police station for questioning and confessed. However, due to international relations, he was immediately released, and only the stolen money was recovered. The Filipino athletes can be said to be quite troublesome. Among the Filipino athletes, the high jump prodigy Tolentino is the most popular among Japanese female students, and he has many girlfriends. His fame is almost universally known because Tolentino achieved an astonishing high jump record of two meters in this competition, only three centimeters short of the world record. He also defeated Japanese athlete Kimura Kazuo, who scored 1.96 meters. In the 7th competition, the high jump record was 1.835 meters, held by Raysa of the Philippines. In the 8th competition, Tolentino broke the record with 1.93 meters. At that time, Kimura Kazuo won the silver medal with 1.90 meters. After returning to his country, he practiced diligently, and last year Kimura achieved a Japanese record of 1.94 meters. At the same time, Tolentino also had a record of 1.94 meters in the Philippines. Both sides had equal strength, and the Japanese were eager to avenge their defeat. Relying on Kimura's courage, they believed they had a better chance of winning. However, during the competition, Tolentino put on an extraordinary performance, and Kimura was defeated. In this competition, the Filipinos only had this one achievement that was barely satisfactory, and Tolentino's reputation soared. On May 27, at a grand reception in Hibiya Park, the Japanese publicly elected Tolentino to represent the Filipino athletes in a speech. Amidst enthusiastic applause, Tolentino said, "In 1927, in Shanghai, China, I received all kinds of preferential treatment from the Chinese, and my performance improved rapidly, reaching a record of 1.93 meters. After returning to my country, the people treated me even better, and my life was comfortable, so my performance improved to 1.94 meters. In this competition, the Japanese hospitality was impeccable, and the food and lodging were excellent, so my performance suddenly jumped to two meters. This is the proof of the facts." The crowd applauded and laughed. Tolentino's words were indeed subtle and double-edged. As for talk of "honey traps," it is really a case of paranoia and an unfair accusation against the Japanese. In track and field, the all-around competition, swimming, baseball, tennis, etc., the Japanese already have a full grasp of the situation and do not need to resort to tricks. In short, the cause of the scandalous affair is based on the Japanese women's psychology of worshiping athletes. There is one benefit and one disadvantage. The excessive promotion of sports by the Japanese government and public has led to the emergence of this kind of phenomenon.

After the distant trees, the evening glow is as beautiful as a picture, with five colors intertwined indescribably. When the glow disappears, the moon rises. The rising of the moon seems to be suppressed, struggling to rise. It first shows its edge, then gradually half of it, and then gradually the whole thing. Its color is like fire, and it is quite large. The higher it rises, the smaller and whiter it becomes. When it no longer shrinks, it is already three or four times smaller than when it first rose. After dinner, I drag a wicker chair and sit under the tree, listening to the old villagers tell ghost stories. Although they are absurd, they are still enjoyable. In this way, I spent a week, drinking wine, with the host and guests not urging each other to drink, stopping when they were satisfied. We also played bamboo war games, no longer remembering who won or lost. Every meal included crabs, which, although not fully grown, were incredibly tender, unlike anything found elsewhere. I was pressed by affairs and regretted how quickly this week passed.

Elegant Talk of Melons by Yan Qian 106

Yan Qian

I once met an old melon farmer who gave me a detailed account of his experience growing melons. I will now record some of the more interesting aspects of his talk to help with summer conversation.

For muskmelons, those fertilized with bean cake are the sweetest, especially those near the main stem. The melons near the main stem are called "first vine melons" and have a particularly sweet taste, but they are not round and symmetrical. The melons further down the vine gradually become rounder and larger, but their taste is definitely inferior to the first vine melons. Good melon sellers often offer the first vine melons to people to try, and people think that because they are small, crooked, and have a particularly good taste, the larger, rounder melons must taste even better, so they choose to buy those. Little do they know that the result is the opposite. Therefore, there is a common saying to describe someone who is short and capable but not particularly attractive in appearance: "first vine melon."

Watermelons, on the other hand, are the opposite of muskmelons. The longer the vine, the sweeter the melons it produces. When watermelons are ripe, they must be turned over so that they are exposed to the sun, so that the entire melon gets even sunlight and the sweetness is also even. The water in the melon field must also be evenly distributed. If it is evenly distributed, the melons will be large and beautiful. Whenever there is damage from rain or wind and wilting vines are found, they should be removed. Otherwise, the wilting disease will spread and hinder the growth of the melons. Small spots and scars on the melons are traces of small flying insects such as gnats sucking and eating. Not only do they not harm the melon, but they are a characteristic of the melon's beauty. Whether it is watermelon or muskmelon, one should pay attention to seeking the beauty of its quality during its production and should not only seek the quantity. Therefore, one should often inspect the rows and remove the redundant melons from time to time, so that the remaining melons will be large and beautiful.

Warmth in My Heart (2) (4) (7) 107

Bao Tianxiao

Chapter Thirteen: Who planted the ring unintentionally? This is the fate. Who sings the golden thread with intention?

The pair of bracelets that Zuo Shichen now possesses are foreign-made, but they are things from a bygone era. They are expandable, spring-loaded bracelets with a small watch embedded in the center. They are made of a metal alloy, and when they were new, they must have been as brilliantly golden as gold itself. It's a pity that the gold plating has been worn away by time, and the exterior has lost its color. This is like a person whose golden age has passed, and who has become an obsolete relic. Judging by these bracelets, it was certainly intended to be a state-of-the-art fashion accessory and certainly not designed to facilitate hand labor. It is a women's fashion item. Later, someone came up with the idea of wearing watches on the wrist, which is very convenient. The bracelet can be said to be a relic of a bygone era. In addition, the silver powder box and gold buttons are ordinary objects and nothing to marvel at. The prize redemption center examined the tickets and handed over the prizes one by one, then closed down. At that time, Zuo Shichen wanted to ask what the first prize was. Shi Guanping said that the first prize had already been claimed: it was a pearl brooch in the shape of a flower basket, said to be worth three thousand dollars. Actually, it was not worth three thousand dollars; it was worth only about sixteen or seventeen hundred dollars. It was said to have been won by a young lady from a mansion, which was fitting; it was like giving a fine sword to a hero. You've won so many things, but none of them are useful to you, so you might as well give them to your wife. Zuo Shichen asked, "I heard that you also donated a lot of paintings and antiques. Why aren't any of them in this lottery?" Shi Guanping replied, "We are a separate group. They are a separate group. We can't mix them together. Their group is all jewelry and valuables; in short, things for women. Originally, we wanted to combine the jewelry and valuables with the paintings and antiques, and then distribute them, for example, with the first two prizes being half jewelry and valuables and half paintings and antiques. But some people disagreed, saying that people who like jewelry and valuables may not like paintings and antiques, and those who like paintings and antiques may not like jewelry and valuables. It would be better to separate them so that people can buy tickets for the prizes they prefer. Coincidentally, the ladies donated so much jewelry that it was enough to hold a lottery, so we decided to hold the 'Planting Fortune' lottery first, which was all for jewelry and valuables. That's why the first prize was a pearl brooch and the second prize was a diamond ring, both things that women need. As for the many paintings and antiques that we collected, we also plan to hold a lottery, with all prizes being paintings and antiques. We don't need to squeeze it in the middle of this meeting; we can hold that lottery whenever we want."

US Cotton Does Not Seek a Bumper Harvest 117

The current situation remains unfavorable.

August weather is important.

A telegram from New York on the first of the month reported on the cotton market conditions for the past week, stating that cotton prices this week have fallen to a new low for the season under the pressure of continued liquidation by Wall Street and selling from the South, as well as reports of continued sluggishness in the textile industry. Although there have been unfavorable reports on the climate and cotton production, they have failed to arouse the interest of traders and speculators, and the general sentiment is increasingly bearish. Rain has been seen recently in the central part of the cotton belt, but it has only reduced some of the drought. Texas and Oklahoma have only had a few light showers, and the high temperatures have not abated. Reports of deteriorating cotton production have increased significantly. Private year-end reports indicate that the average condition of new cotton crops is currently 66.7% of normal, which may result in a harvest of approximately 14,182,000 bales. It is said that buying interest rose slightly when prices fell, because cotton prices were lower than the average cost of production, and it is believed that if the weather in August remains dry and hot, the overall situation may change rapidly.

Furthermore, it is reported that rain has been seen in various parts of the Southwest, but the rainfall is insufficient. If the drought and heat are not reduced immediately, the damage in the Southwest will be significant. General trade is poor, especially in textiles. There will inevitably be more supply for hedging sales in the future, so the market sentiment is bearish. Speakers still say that only a normal cotton production is needed at present. Shigemitsu Kicks Back Against Japanese Warships Coming to China 125

Yesterday, according to sources at the Japanese Legation Office, the Japanese government's Ministry of the Navy, citing the Chinese Xiang Rebellion, dispatched a number of warships to China to protect Japanese nationals. After receiving the order, the fleet had already prepared all the procedures for departure, awaiting orders to move out. Although there was a slight disturbance in Hunan Province, other places were extremely safe, and the National Government had dispatched a large number of troops to suppress the rebellion, which could be quelled within days. There was no need to dispatch troops and warships in such a commotion, which would provide an excuse for diplomatic relations. Therefore, in addition to going to Beijing to exchange opinions, he had telegraphed back to the Japanese government to inform them of the actual situation, so that the Japanese government could understand the truth and stop the Japanese navy from acting rashly.

Progress of Various Circles in Preparing for the Construction of Sun Yat-sen's Bronze Statue 128

According to the Guowen News Agency, the proposal by various circles in Shanghai to build a bronze statue of Sun Yat-sen at the North Railway Station was initiated in 1928. At that time, the Shanghai-Nanjing-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration and the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, the Municipal Government, and the Songhu Garrison Command jointly suggested that various agencies and organizations in Shanghai join and organize the Shanghai North Railway Station Construction Sun Yat-sen Bronze Statue Committee. It was decided that the construction cost would be 30,000 yuan, and a donation booklet would be printed and distributed to various agencies to raise funds. The base of the bronze statue had already been laid in the open space in front of the Shanghai North Railway Station Bureau. Over the years, it has been affected by the current situation and personnel changes, and the person in charge has lacked the ability to carry it out, which has led to delays. Since this year, the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, the Songhu Garrison Command, the Shanghai Municipal Government, and the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration have repeatedly convened representatives of various agencies to meet and discuss ways to continue the work and expedite its implementation in the shortest possible time. Therefore, the Shanghai All Circles Construction Sun Yat-sen Bronze Statue Preparatory Committee was reorganized and held meetings to actively prepare. Another donation booklet was printed and distributed to various agencies to be responsible for soliciting donations. The funds raised were sent directly by the fundraising agencies to the Shanghai Commercial & Savings Bank for storage and receipts were issued. Later, the donations collected amounted to more than 20,000 yuan, so the conference discussed and decided to proceed with the construction. However, since the various agencies were scattered in various places for business, it was extremely inconvenient, so the meeting decided to elect more than a dozen construction committee members and then elect five standing committee members from the construction committee to be responsible for the work, namely, Ye Xiufu, representative of the Shanghai Municipal Party Department, Zhang Taiji, representative of the Songhu Garrison Command, Lin Yan, representative of the Shanghai Municipal Government, Wang Jinzhi and Wang Chunbai, representatives of the Nanjing-Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railway Administration, Zheng Fusang, and Wang Xiaolai, a well-known businessman. Since the establishment of the construction committee, the standing committee members have decided on every step of the construction by first soliciting drawings of Sun Yat-sen's bronze statue and engineering plans, and then having the committee review whether they are appropriate to decide whether to adopt them and modify them, and then decide on the subsequent course of action. It is because Sun Yat-sen's achievements in the party and the country were outstanding throughout the ages, and the training of respecting achievements and repaying virtue was taken as an example for making gold and casting statues. It is not only the view of the capital city, but also the glory of thousands of years. The drawings and engineering plans for this statue must be carefully selected for adoption in order to show respect. Therefore, on June 5 this year, a special announcement was published in the Shenbao, News News, Shishi News, and the Republic of China Daily to solicit applications widely. It is heard that there are quite a few applicants. The statutory period for accepting the drawings is limited to one week, ending on June 11, and no invitation for bids was published. It is now heard that the committee members attach great importance to this matter. All proposals are not only made with great care, but also all matters are decided by public vote. The reviewers have signed the responsible review report, and the report's opinions must still be thoroughly discussed and decided by the entire committee to determine adoption. It is heard that the committee members said that the organization of this public group is entirely composed of all circles in Shanghai, and it is a matter of commemorating Sun Yat-sen's merits and establishing a bronze statue. All the funds are donated by the public. If it is not to insult Sun Yat-sen and violate the dignity of the party, and other non-Jiang actions, and there is solid evidence, one or two committee members in the meeting cannot control it, let alone be manipulated by external slander, and no one can destroy it.

Overseas Chinese Remittances Home Each Year 129

Recent surveys show over 400 million yuan.

Losses due to silver devaluation will diminish in the future.

The Statistics Department of the Legislative Yuan, in order to address the issue of gold appreciation and silver devaluation, has recently sent personnel to Shanghai to investigate the state of international finance over the past sixty years. According to a survey, the exact amount of remittances from overseas Chinese to China each year is over 400 million yuan. It is divided into two parts: one is savings and interest in Chinese banks, and the other is investment in domestic industry and commerce to revitalize national products. Overseas Chinese remittances home are all remitted in gold pounds from their countries of residence. When they arrive in Shanghai, they are converted into silver yuan according to the market price. Since the issue of gold appreciation and silver devaluation has occurred, the savings of general overseas Chinese have suffered greatly. If our country does not quickly implement a gold exchange standard to remedy the situation, there are fears that future remittances from overseas Chinese will diminish.

Japanese Merchants Dominate Food Supplies in North China 130

Japanese Ships Transport Rice, Japanese Factories Grind Wheat

Since the Jianghai Customs prohibited the transportation of food to various ports in North China by Japanese ships, the Shanghai side has not allowed the shipment of white rice, flour, and other items to Weihaiwei, Yantai, and Tianjin. A large number of foreign rice was blocked in Shanghai in late last month, as reported in this newspaper. However, there is a great shortage of food in the north, and the people's livelihood has also caused panic. The Jianghai Customs generally refuses to close customs for those who report the shipment of food. Recently, it has been confirmed that a certain Japanese shipping company in this port has sent ships to carry a large amount of foreign rice directly to Tianjin, and the first batch of 2,000 bags was loaded and shipped the day before yesterday. A second batch of foreign rice will be transported in the near future. Japanese merchants are acting as agents for wheat flour. The sales of Beiyang wheat flour are very large. Since the Ministry of Finance of the National Government ordered the prohibition of flour exports, southern wheat flour has no way to ship out. It is heard that the north is contracting with Japanese wheat flour manufacturers to use various factories to transport wheat to Japan for grinding into flour and then transport it to Tianjin, and also to purchase 200,000 dan of foreign flour from Japan to meet urgent needs. Recently, there has been a lot of foreign flour loaded onto ships in Shanghai for Tianjin. Various shipping companies are competing to solicit shipments. The freight rate, which used to be 18 cents per dan, has now been reduced by Taikoo by 9 cents first, a decrease of half the original price. On average, each bag of flour only costs 3 cents for the water foot (transportation fee), because three bags make up one dan. Chinese and Japanese merchant ships have also followed suit and lowered prices.

The Yingchang Labor Strike is Resolved 132

Workers Resume Work Today

Officials Send Police to Protect

The labor strike at the Yingchang Factory of the Greater China Match Company in Lujia Ferry, Pudong, was caused by the dismissal of one worker. The various agencies have sent people to mediate many times without a decision. Yesterday morning at 9:00, the Social Bureau, together with the Municipal Party Department, invited representatives from both labor and capital to the bureau to discuss the matter again. Seven labor representatives, including Cao Shenyun, He Guitang, and Wu Xingxiang, and two capital representatives, Mr. Qian and Mr. Qi, attended the meeting. At the same time, two staff representatives, Zhang Zili and Zhang Meichun, were also elected to attend. The labor side first put forward conditions, requesting that eight workers, including Zhu Jinshu, Xue Jinshu, Wang Jinpei, Zhou Longer, Lu Koulong, Zhao Yukui, Liu Chunlin, and Zhu Hongbiao, who had been detained by the Public Security Bureau, be released first, and that Tong Zhaosan, who had been laid off, be restored to work. The Greater China Company should give a corresponding retirement salary for the dismissal during the strike period. After repeated discussions by the mediators, the conditions are that the workers of the factory did not obtain the consent of the authorities before the strike, which is an illegal act. Considering the ignorance of the workers, they should first resume work as a prerequisite, and then discuss the conditions related to labor-capital relations. As for the eight workers who were arrested, they are suspected of other cases and are not involved in the scope of labor-capital relations. They must be judged by law before deciding whether to release them. The labor side agreed and signed the agreement on the spot, and notified the workers to resume work at 3:00 in the morning (today). At that time, the staff representatives also made a request, stating that on the day the labor strike was launched, they were hungry in the factory for a day until the Public Security Bureau rescued them in the evening. Hu asked the Public Security Bureau to send police to protect the security when they entered the factory after resuming work. The Public Security Bureau representatives who attended the meeting agreed to first gather all the staff in the Pudong Third District Office at 8:00 am today and then酌派長警 protect them to enter the factory and serve.

French Water and Electricity Labor Strike Yesterday's News 134

General Assembly: The French Water and Electricity Workers' Union held a general meeting of all members at the Daji Road Public Sports Field at 3:00 pm yesterday. More than 1,400 people attended. The Municipal Party Department specially sent representatives Zhang Yunqing, Hu Shouqi, and Zhao Zhenhui, representatives of the Shanghai Municipal Trade Union Support Association, to attend and guide the meeting. Zhang Amao was publicly elected as the chairman. After the ceremony, the chairman first reported on the purpose of the meeting and the tough attitude of the capital side, which could not be approached for mediation. Since the start of the labor strike, nearly 40 people have been forced by the factory to go on strike due to the oppression of imperialism. All the workers could no longer bear it and requested that all circles give practical assistance and unite in the spirit of fighting externally. Then, Xu Amei spoke in succession to discuss and decide on important cases as follows: (1) For the July 21 tragedy, the French authorities are requested to formally apologize to this meeting, and the resolution was unanimously passed by all. (2) All staff in the company's comprador office are required to report to the meeting today. (3) How should we deal with the workers in the car department who are scabs and drive trams out of the factory to undermine strike discipline? The resolution was unanimously resolved to deal with all of them. (4) In the future, the news of meetings of the car affairs, mechanical affairs, and staff departments will be merged and published in a unified manner. (5) It is decided that a joint meeting of the strike committee and the picketing team will be convened at the association at 9:00 am tomorrow (the 3rd) to discuss the method of proceeding.

Staff Meeting: The staff meeting was held at 10:00 am. 230 staff members attended the meeting. Zhang Renjun was publicly elected as the chairman. The chairman then reported that the staff support association had sent representatives to contact the matter, saying that he had heard that the company was planning to hire Westerners to replace the positions, which was not true. The representatives had made a clear statement that the company had no such intention. As for the mediation, he heard that the capital side was currently in contact with the consuls, etc. The general result could be satisfactory, and the comprador himself was also trying his best to find a way to eliminate the labor strike as soon as possible, and asked him to make concessions and not insist on the previous agreement. Subsequently, Yan Baoshu, Zhu Yonghua, Fan Baokun, Dai Molin, Feng Shenglin, and others spoke in succession, and their words were very sincere. Finally, the extension of the strike was discussed. It is heard that a proper method has been raised.

Notice from the Support Association: Notice No. 53 from the Shanghai Municipal Trade Union Support French Water and Electricity Workers' Union regarding the announcement of the matter. The labor strike of French water and electricity in this city has been prolonged without a decision. All the details of the matter are known. However, the various committees of this association are organized by the election of various trade unions, but the ability is limited. I am sincerely afraid that it will be difficult to do. Therefore, it is specifically scheduled to convene a general meeting of representatives of all trade unions in the city at 1:00 pm on the 6th of this month on the third floor of the Municipal Party Department to gather the strength of the group to jointly plan for the method of dealing with the matter. In addition to formally requesting the Municipal Party Department to send personnel to attend and guide the meeting, Mr. Li Shizeng, a member of the Central Committee, is also invited to attend the meeting to report on the progress of the mediation. At that time, I hope that your association will send representatives to attend the meeting to express their opinions and jointly plan the course of action. This is very important.

The Municipal Social Affairs Bureau issued an order to the Trade Union, saying that it was an order to comply with the law. The case was based on the Municipal Government's Order No. 5204, which stated that the French Concession authorities' labor strike has been disrupted and there is still no solution. This matter has been repeatedly negotiated between the Yong with the French Concession authorities and the workers in order to settle the matter. The situation is as follows: yesterday, I met with the French Consul General and received a firm entrustment to resolve the matter as soon as possible. Yong is obliged to do so, but he is deeply concerned that it will be difficult to recover the situation. All parties must sincerely help each other to avoid undermining the cause. I beg you to advise the workers to remain calm and wait for a solution. Do not act impulsively to avoid causing additional problems and expanding the trend. As for the fact that the Municipal Party Department's Civil Training Committee is also very cautious about this labor strike, whether it should be transferred to the Municipal Party Department for proper handling and to resolve the problems in an invisible manner, and whether you should inform them to work together to adjust and clarify the sub-items to achieve twice the result with half the effort, I hope you will make a wise decision and also show your reply, etc., in addition to replying to continue to work to resolve the dispute as soon as possible, and also inform the Civil Training Committee to cooperate in adjusting, clarify, and order that the Bureau should immediately investigate and transfer the order to the labor side to wait quietly for a solution.

Establishment of the Preparatory Committee of the Shanghai Yarn Factory Industry Workers' Union 135

The preparatory committee of the Shanghai Yarn Factory Industry Workers' Union held its first meeting yesterday at the Xihe Yarn Factory Workers' Union. Huang Huanan, Wang Ruiting, Zhou Zhonghua, Zhou Ziyang, and others attended, with Xu Shaochuan as the instructor. The following matters were resolved: (1) Regarding the assignment of duties, it was decided to appoint Zhou Ziyang, Li Changgen, and Ju Xizhang as standing committee members, with Zhou Zhonghua and Wang Ruiting as the director and deputy director of the guidance section, and Huang Huanan and Wu Fuxing as the director and deputy director of the registration section. (2) The proposal to appoint Bao Ziheng, Long Yunfeng, and Cai Keguang as staff members of the union was approved. (3) The proposal to appoint Chen Zhongrou as secretary and Wu Yuchen as recorder was approved. (4) The union decided to commence operations on August 3rd. (5) (Omitted). (6) Publish a declaration. (7) Prepare a budget statement for convenient disbursement, which was decided to be handled by the standing committee members. (8) The use of the official seal should be reported to the higher authorities for record. (9) A request should be submitted to the Public Training Association for a letter to the Public Security Bureau and the political department of the Public Concession, requesting enhanced protection for the union's staff. (10) The union's regular meeting date should be decided, and it was resolved to hold it every Sunday. The meeting adjourned. The declaration of the establishment of the preparatory committee of the Shanghai Yarn Factory Industry Workers' Union reads: To all levels of Party departments, organizations, labor unions, and compatriots across the nation, since the late Premier founded the revolution, adopted the Three Principles of the People, and sought the liberation of weak and small ethnic groups and the slogan of overthrowing imperialism, the people, who were under heavy oppression and on the verge of death, all rose up to support the revolution, seeking their own liberation and overthrowing the oppression of imperialism and capitalists. Therefore, before the revolutionary army arrived, the people had already organized groups to welcome the revolution with incense and flowers and assist in eliminating warlords. Among them, our laboring workers were the most powerful because the greater the oppression, the stronger the resistance. It is a natural principle that workers are willing to sacrifice, fearless of hardship, and go through fire and water with a spirit of fearlessness to fulfill their responsibility as revolutionaries. This is also due to the unbearable oppression of capitalism and imperialism during the Manchu autocratic era. In all matters, it is important to have a beginning and an end and to seek thoroughness to achieve good results. Reflecting on the late Premier's revolution, it took ten failures to overthrow the Manchu Qing Dynasty, abolish autocracy, and establish the foundation of the Republic of China. If at that time the determination was not firm and there was a slight discouragement, how could the great cause of the revolution have succeeded? Now, using the Premier's revolution as an analogy to our workers' movement, the workers' movement belongs to the workers' revolution. Whoever is on the workers' side, who does not sympathize and who is not excited? Thus, the substantial strength of the workers' movement is evident. It is regrettable that Chinese workers are discouraged before failing and arrogant before succeeding. This common problem within themselves creates numerous obstacles for the future. Not only will it fail to promote success, but it will also lead to a dead end. The nation's industry is declining day by day, and the suffering of workers is increasing day by day. As the saying goes, "The boatman digs a hole in his own boat," which is truly not false. This is truly heartbreaking for the trajectory of the Chinese workers' movement and unfortunate for the future of the nation. However, as the ancients said, "To err and not correct is to err indeed." Now that we know the past mistakes of the Chinese workers' movement, we should correct them and continue to strive for the realization of liberation. This is not only fortunate for the workers of the whole country but also fortunate for the future of the nation. In the past, the Shanghai workers' movement was controlled by the Communist Party and manipulated by politicians, resulting in fragmentation and chaos. The workers' knowledge is limited, and they are at a loss and easily mistake the enemy for their father and make unnecessary sacrifices to be used as tools by these people. Moreover, there is no way to alleviate their own suffering. The workers' strength is dispersed, and the organization is lax, resulting in self-cannibalization and countless malpractices. If it is like this in a big port, the situation in other areas can be imagined. This time, the Municipal Party Department, based on the trade union law promulgated by the Central Government, has ordered the establishment of industry-wide federations. This industry has been ordered to establish the preparatory committee of the Shanghai Yarn Factory Industry Workers' Union. The union silently remembers the importance of the entrusted task and the eagerness for improvement, so it intends to propose several guidelines: (1) Organize and consolidate the trade unions in the industry. There are no less than dozens of cotton yarn factories in this city, and nearly ten have trade union organizations, while the majority still do not have organizations. The union intends to consolidate those that already have organizations to make them sound, and send personnel to guide the organization of those that have not been organized, so that the industry has a sound organization, and all workers are on the right track, seeking the liberation of workers under the leadership of the Party and helping the development of the disaster relief industry. (2) Eliminate the Communist Party. Shanghai is a place where Chinese and foreigners live together, and the concessions are adjacent to each other, making it easy for the Communist Party to hide. There are often incidents of inciting workers and agitating for strikes, which not only destroy the workers' movement but also hinder social security. The union will strictly investigate and prevent loyal workers from being deceived. (3) Implement labor-capital cooperation. It is found that the oppression suffered by Chinese workers from domestic capitalists is small, and the greatest oppression is from imperialism. Because China has been subjected to political and economic aggression, the Chinese proletariat has no place to stand. If we do not seek a fundamental solution, it will be useless. In the future, the union should abide by the late Premier's teachings, adopt a near-sighted and far-reaching strategy, first find a way to eliminate the aggression of imperialism, increase Chinese production, improve industry, consolidate the foundation of the nation, and the liberation of workers will have a good way. The above points are only a summary of the major ones. In short, the union aims to unite forces to seek the liberation of workers and strive for the survival of the nation. Under the leadership of the Party, it will work hard for the workers' movement. Anyone who destroys the workers or undermines the workers' movement will be dealt with with all our strength without leniency. It is hoped that compatriots from all walks of life will provide guidance and make up for our shortcomings to complete our mission. This declaration is made.

Strike at the Pudong Rihua Yarn Factory 136

Declaration of Assistance from Various Trade Unions in Pudong

The Shanghai British-American Tobacco Factory Union, the Shanghai Xiang Sheng Iron Factory Union, the Shanghai Taikoo Shanbei Steamboat Loading and Unloading Union, the Shanghai Yingchang Match Factory Union, the Shanghai Pudong Construction Union, the Shanghai Pudong Porter Union, the Shanghai Pudong Garment Union, and others issued a declaration yesterday stating that over 3,000 workers from the seven Rihua Textile Unions in Pudong have had a glorious history in the past revolutionary journey. However, in recent years, the union affairs have been controlled by a small number of labor traitors and running dogs who have helped the Japanese imperialist capitalists oppress the workers and completely sold out the union, causing the workers to suffer unspeakable miseries. According to what we know, among the over 3,000 workers in the Rihua Yarn Factory, over 1,000 are temporary workers. Because the wages of temporary workers are the lowest and no rice allowance is given, several wages and rice allowances can be saved each month. There are often cases where people who have been in the factory for one or two years are still working as temporary workers. They recruit as many temporary workers as possible and squeeze out as many permanent workers as possible, making everyone feel insecure and have to obey orders. This is the first point. The Rihua Yarn Factory has over 2,000 workers, which is not a small number. Labor-capital conditions have never been signed. Even if there are occasional local disputes, the resolutions made by the Party and government agencies are completely overturned by the factory and none are implemented. This is the second point. The central government stipulates long-term holidays. All Chinese and foreign factories have strictly followed this rule. The Pudong British-American factory stops work for 11 days each year, and the Xiang Sheng factory stops work for 14 days each year. The factory pays wages and rice allowances as usual. However, the Rihua Yarn Factory does not have this kind of treatment. This is the third point. Gold is expensive and silver is cheap, and prices are soaring. Other Chinese and foreign factories have voluntarily increased wages. The Rihua workers, who have the lowest wages, are naturally unable to make a living. However, the factory not only refuses to increase wages but also fines workers for even the slightest mistake. The fines are always several times higher than the wages. If you open the factory's fine book, it is truly heartbreaking. Each month, the entire factory is fined at least several thousand yuan or more. This kind of fine is the same as the temporary workers, which is a way to deduct wages and exploit workers. I am afraid that there is no such harsh example in all Chinese and foreign factories in the city and the country. This is the fourth point. The Rihua Yarn Factory has to work 11 and a half hours every day, and only half an hour for lunch is the rest time. The factory also increases the workload. The number of teeth in the fine yarn machine is increased from 36 to 54, and the speed of the machine is extremely fast. The factory only knows about production and does not care about the lives of the workers. This is the fifth point. The above are just a few of the known oppressions, and it is difficult to enumerate the other oppressions. Just from this small sample, we can see the ferocious face of the Japanese imperialist capitalists and the ruthless heart of the labor traitors and running dogs who trample on the workers. It can also prove that the demands of all the workers in the Rihua Yarn Factory this time, such as paying wages on commemorative days, increasing rice allowances, shortening the time for leave, not delaying deductions from wages, and stopping night work on Sundays in summer, are not excessive at all. Now that the factory has rejected the workers' minimum demands, after the strike, it is listening to the instigation of the labor traitors and running dogs to expel loyal workers. The party and government mediation has been repeatedly rejected. The trade unions believe that the Rihua Yarn Factory's treatment of the workers is not only unbearable for the Rihua workers but also fears that this trend will be followed by other factories, and the entire interests of the workers will be destroyed. Therefore, on the one hand, we expose the various inhumane atrocities of the Rihua Yarn Factory capitalists in oppressing the workers with facts, and on the other hand, we unite the 800,000 workers in the city to help the striking workers in the Rihua Yarn Factory to get rid of the unequal shackles and allow the more than 3,000 oppressed compatriots to strive for the final victory and restore their human status from a non-human status, so that we can fulfill our responsibility. (Omitted below)

The ministry now intends to consult with various relevant submarine and wireless telegraph companies to actively reduce the price of international news telegrams to facilitate the dissemination of information. Shigemitsu's Speech Before Going to Beijing 139

Foreigners Need Not Panic Unnecessarily

Japanese Acting Minister to China Shigemitsu Aoi received an urgent telegram from the Foreign Ministry of his government the day before yesterday (the 1st), instructing him to travel to Beijing by night train at 11 pm, accompanied by Secretary Hayashi, Secretary Nomura, and Secretary Asahina, to meet with Foreign Minister Wang and Acting Chairman Tan to discuss methods to protect the security of Japanese nationals in the Hunan and Hubei areas and exchange various opinions on handling the aftermath. He is scheduled to return to Shanghai next week. According to his temporary statement, "This time, I am instructed by my government to go to Beijing to meet with Foreign Minister Wang and others to discuss the security protection of Japanese nationals in Hunan and Hubei. There is no other meaning besides exchanging opinions. Although the bandit-communist incident in Hunan Province is extremely serious, I firmly believe that the National Government has the ability to guard against and suppress it and will soon be able to quell it and make the outside world safe from danger. Therefore, in my opinion, foreigners must not panic unnecessarily to avoid disturbing themselves. After I arrive in Beijing, I will stay in Beijing for a few days due to the summer heat and plan to return to Shanghai via Yongdao next week." Judging from Mr. Shigemitsu's attitude, he is very calm. As for the rumors that the Japanese have formally lodged a protest, it is a misunderstanding.

Six Measures to Suppress Superstition 143

The Municipal Government Orders the Public Security Bureau to Comply

After the Shanghai Municipal Government approved the Ministry of Interior's request to prohibit divination and geomancy, it immediately ordered the Public Security Bureau to comply. The details of the suppression measures are recorded as follows: (1) All local diviners, astrologers, witches, geomancers, and others who engage in business by spreading superstition shall be forced to change to other legitimate occupations within three months of the announcement. (2) After the local Public Security Bureau announces the measures, it shall convene local diviners, astrologers, witches, geomancers, and others to explain the disadvantages of superstition in detail and urge them to realize their errors and change their occupations on schedule. (3) Those who have not found a legitimate occupation after the deadline shall be admitted to local factories and ordered to learn a skill within a limited time. In areas where no factories have been established, they may be ordered to undertake appropriate work. Those who are truly old, weak, disabled, or ill shall be admitted to local relief homes or other appropriate measures shall be taken. (4) If anyone continues to engage in business in violation of the order after the deadline, the police shall be ordered to stop their business immediately. (5) All local bookstores and bookstores that publish or sell books on divination, astrology, witchcraft, geomancy, etc., and other books that spread superstition shall also be prohibited. (6) In all cases of marriage, funeral, and illness, the people shall not be allowed to employ diviners, astrologers, witches, geomancers, etc. to pray for good fortune or tell fortunes. Those who violate this rule shall be stopped and punished.

It was agreed to donate from June 1st

Sand fishing boats entering and leaving Wusong from Tongchonghai and other areas should pay boat donations to the Boat Donation Office of the Municipal Finance Bureau in accordance with the regulations. However, boat owners have been claiming that sand fishing boats are different from other types of boats and have not complied with the donation rates set by the Municipal Finance Bureau. Now, the new director of the Finance Bureau, Mr. Tang Naikang, is actively rectifying the donation affairs and pays great attention to this case. After receiving the order, the staff members have cleared the boat donations with the Wusong Chamber of Commerce and the Wusong Chamber of Commerce has convened representatives of various sand fishing boat owners to negotiate and agree to pay in accordance with the regulations and to set June 1st as the date to start donating.

The Authorities Encourage Smokers to Surrender Themselves 146

Designate a Concurrent Opium Rehabilitation Hospital

The Municipal Health and Public Security Bureaus were instructed by the Municipal Government to designate hospitals that concurrently handle opium rehabilitation matters and establish opium rehabilitation centers. They will send the arrested opium addicts to the hospital to be forced to quit. They are also afraid that the general public of opium addicts are not fully aware of the opium rehabilitation measures and are afraid to move forward, which would be a loss to the central government's spirit of encouraging opium addicts to surrender themselves and quit opium. Therefore, the two bureaus jointly issued a notice on the previous day, stating: For the purpose of the notice, the case was approved by the Municipal Government's 4787th instruction, in which the case was approved by the Anti-Opium Committee to inquire about the hospitals that have been designated to concurrently handle opium rehabilitation matters, the establishment of the city and county opium rehabilitation centers, and the sending of arrested opium addicts to the hospital to be forced to quit. They are also afraid that the general public of opium addicts are not fully aware of the opium rehabilitation measures and are afraid to move forward, which would be a loss to the spirit of the central government's establishment of opium rehabilitation hospitals to encourage opium addicts to surrender themselves and quit opium. In accordance with Article 16 of the Regulations for the Implementation of Anti-Opium Law, opium addicts who voluntarily surrender themselves and are willing to be admitted to the hospital to quit opium or quit opium before being discovered shall be exempt from punishment. The decision was made at the 39th committee meeting of the association and inquired to the governments of all provinces and special cities to announce it to the public so that opium addicts can have the opportunity to voluntarily surrender themselves and be admitted to the hospital to quit opium. In addition to the separate inquiries, the case was recorded and inquired for investigation and compliance, and I hope that you will instruct your subordinates to comply, etc. In addition to the separate orders, the order is hereby ordered to the bureaus to comply and jointly announce it to the public. The list of hospitals that have been designated to handle opium rehabilitation is attached as follows: Public Shanghai Hospital, San Tai Pier, Nanshi; Chinese Red Cross General Hospital, Haige Road, Concession; Southeast Hospital, Hujunying, Nanshi; Civilian Hospital, Xinjiang Road, Zhabei; Jiangsu Opium Rehabilitation Hospital, Zhizaoju Road, Nanshi.

Three Notices from the Car Affairs Office of Two Railways 148

The Car Affairs Office of the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways issued three notices to all station staff on the railways yesterday: (1) The Shanghai-Hangzhou Railway has been testing the use of full-train braking air pipes for freight cars Nos. 25 and 26. According to regulations, at least one air pipe must be installed on every four freight cars. This has been implemented since July 16th. After the train arrives at each terminal station, the station master must, together with the brakeman and the car shop inspector, test whether the air pipe is flexible and applicable before the train departs, and record the results of the test in detail for future reference. (2) In order to facilitate the engineering office to have sufficient time before the train to arrange for loading and unloading materials at each station, after the materials are loaded on the train, the station of departure should first fill out the notification before it is determined which train to hang it on. When it is determined which train to hang it on, the train number should be telegraphed. The transportation of these materials should be assisted by the dispatching department to the greatest extent possible to speed up the loading and hanging of the train, and the car should be quickly transferred back to be used for adjustment after the car is empty. Please abide by it. (3) It has been found that train personnel must wear uniforms when on duty. This is a final warning. Anyone who has already received a uniform must wear it when on duty. If there is any violation, the chief of the car affairs section will immediately report it for punishment without leniency.

Results of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau's Relief Efforts for the Town of Zhenjiang's Cattle Plague 149

Last month, a cattle plague broke out in the villages in the Fourth District of Zhenjiang, Qianbei Township. The plague was so rampant that more than 200 cattle died within a few days. The villagers were very panicked and specially submitted a report to the Jiangsu Agricultural and Mining Department requesting that measures be taken to provide relief. The department considered that the Livestock and Product Inspection Office of the Shanghai Commodity Inspection Bureau had produced cattle plague serum with good results and provided treatment. It specially commissioned Mr. Zhang Zhenlin to come to Shanghai to contact the bureau. The bureau appointed technician Shou Biao to carry the cattle plague serum to assist the department in injecting it. From July 11th to 18th, the serum was used to inject and treat cattle in various places such as Qianbei Township, Lu Village, Shangluo Village, and Yugan Village in the district. A total of 22 cattle were injected with serum and more than 30 cattle were treated with other methods. A total of more than 50 cattle were cured and the plague was suppressed. The villagers were very grateful. It is reported that the cattle plague serum produced by the bureau is not only purchased by dairy farms near Shanghai, but also by people from as far away as Beijing and Guangzhou who have sent letters to purchase it. Since the demand is high, the production should be increased. Therefore, the bureau is now trying to expand its production capacity to cope with the situation.

The Largest Liner in the Pacific is About to Arrive 158

Changxing's Empress of Japan

Scheduled for Public Viewing on the 9th

In order to compete in the Pacific shipping industry, the Changxing Steamship Company specially built a new, largest, and fastest mail ship in the UK for 2 million gold pounds (equivalent to 36.7 million Chinese dollars). It is named the "Empress of Japan" with a displacement of 33,000 tons and a speed of over 23 knots per hour. The ship is divided into nine layers, and its speed, carrying capacity, passenger capacity, and layout are unprecedented in the Far East. It is the largest of all mail ships in the Pacific. The ship has been completed and sailed from London. According to the telegram received yesterday, it is scheduled to arrive in Shanghai on the 9th of this month. Due to the huge size of the ship and its deep draft, it will be berthed at the Puxi Blue Funnel Wharf. A small launch will be sent to the Xinguang Wharf to welcome people from all walks of life to visit the ship that afternoon. It is reported that Minister of Communications Wang Boqun has also been invited. Refreshments will be provided on board. The ship is scheduled to depart on its maiden voyage to Wen Gu Wu on the 10th.

Chen Yongkang Escapes Danger 159

The Maternal Uncle Was the Mastermind

Relatives Are Truly Unreliable

Chen Yongkang, a four-year-old boy from Huzhou, living at No. 2, Baohua Fang, Huanghe Road, French Concession, was kidnapped and hidden by bandits on the 20th of last month. Afterwards, letters were repeatedly received from the bandits demanding a ransom of 150,000 yuan. It was agreed to negotiate at Ningbo Road, French Concession, at around 8 PM the day before yesterday. However, the matter was discovered by Jin Jiulin, a Chinese detective of the French Concession Police Station. He also used a ruse, disguising himself as a hawker with Vice Detective Mao Jingen and detectives from the robbery squad. He secretly followed Luo Henglin (the maternal uncle of the kidnapped child), who was sent by the Chen family to negotiate. When the time came, three men wearing summer cloth gowns were arrested. The three men confessed that Luo Henglin was the mastermind of the case. Therefore, they were taken to the police station together for strict questioning. They then confessed that Song Hesheng, a Yancheng native, was hiding in Gu's residence at No. 309, Yingchun Fang, Hubei Road. Song was immediately arrested. The details have been reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that after Song was arrested, the location of the kidnapped child was discovered. West Detective Bardi, along with all the detectives, immediately went to the Gordun Road Police Station. The head of the station immediately dispatched several detectives to No. 444, Wuding Fang, Wuding Road, at 3:20 AM yesterday. They rescued the kidnapped child in the shed and arrested the guards, Zhou A'er (18 years old, Sichuan native) and Chang Guang (16 years old, Guangdong native), on the spot. However, no guns were found in the house. The bandits and the kidnapped child were taken to the French Concession Police Station. The family was notified to take the kidnapped child home. The arrested criminals will be sent to the public court for strict investigation.

A Rustic Fool Wearing a Padded Jacket and Carrying a Fake Gun 160

Claiming the Fake Gun Was Enough to Ward Off Evil

Appears to Be Suffering from a Nervous Disorder

Han Qingtai, a policeman at Post No. 37 of the Gaochangmiao Police Station of the Second District General Station of the Public Security Bureau, and patrolling policeman Han Qingyuan, were on duty in front of the Shanghai Army Fire Brigade at 3:25 AM yesterday. Because a special curfew was announced for the previous two nights and it was late at night, all pedestrians were checked. While the two policemen were patrolling, they suddenly saw a man walking from the west. He was wearing a felt hat and a short padded jacket, looking like a rustic fool. The two policemen went forward to check and found a six-inch revolver fake gun on his body. The model was no different from the real one. Two iron tubes and a pedicure knife were also found in his pocket. He was immediately taken to the station and transferred to the general station. After interrogation by District Chief Wang, he confessed that his name was Wang Diwu, a Songjiang native, 40 years old, currently living with relatives outside Xiaonanmen or lodging in small inns. He also claimed that the fake gun he was carrying was purchased from Yimiao during the first month of the lunar year and was carried on his body to ward off evil. The rest of his words were evasive. District Chief Wang heard that this person was wearing a padded jacket and a felt hat in the hot summer and that his speech was erratic, suggesting that he was suffering from a nervous disorder. However, because he was walking at night during the curfew with a fake gun, there were concerns that he might have other motives. He was immediately transferred to the judicial section for review.

Russian Man Shoots Portuguese Man 161

Steals Car and Escapes

Arrested in the French Concession

The Damei Evening News reports that Portuguese man Lu Lailuo of the Jianghai Customs, who lives on Hague Road, took a car to Hongqiao Road last night for business. On the way back, about two miles from the Kaufman General Assembly Hall, a car stopped in front of him, obstructing his driving. It was about 9:30 PM, and it was already dark. As soon as the Portuguese man's car stopped, a man jumped out of the darkness and asked to borrow an air pump. The Portuguese man said he didn't have one and invited him to get in the car and go to a certain place to borrow one. Before he could finish speaking, the man took out a gun and shot at the Portuguese man. Then he tried to shoot the driver. The driver was terrified and ran wildly into the fields. The man failed to catch him and returned to the car, driving at full speed towards the French Concession. The Portuguese man reported the incident to the French Concession Police Station, which immediately dispatched detectives to investigate. About four hours later, the Russian man Chai Valin and his friend Esaike were arrested at No. 532, Avenue Joffre. 102 bullets of various types, a magazine, and three customs badges were found in their car. However, the gun used to shoot the Portuguese man was not on his person. He confessed that he had thrown it away on the way. The Portuguese man's injury was only a graze from the bullet on his left chest muscles, and it was not serious.

Two People Jump into the Huangpu River Due to Economic Pressure 162

Fortunately, Both Were Rescued

Cai Yongde, at the Chunjiang Pier No. 6 ferry in Pudong, on the evening of the day before yesterday at around 5 PM, was loading passengers on the opposite side of the Hankou Road Xinguang Pier and sailing back to Pudong. Just as he arrived in the middle of the river, a passenger with a sad face was about to commit suicide by jumping into the river. Fortunately, a fellow passenger, who claimed to be Wu Yu, working at the High Court, noticed and grabbed him at the critical moment, preventing him from falling into the water. He was escorted to the water patrol police station by the old man Qingyuan. According to his confession, his name is Cai Yongde, and he is 30 years old. He has been married for eight years and has two sons. More than ten years ago, his father worked as a runner at the Xiangtai Lumber Mill in Yangshupu and saved a little money. He bought land in Zhabei Qiujiang Road and built five houses. After his mother died, he remarried to Wang, who soon became estranged from the young couple. Five years ago, they started a small family at No. 898, Jiuruli, Qiujiang Road, upstairs of the Xingyuan South-North Goods Store. He was born as a Western clerk at HSBC Bank and has now been promoted to a small cashier. Although his monthly income is not too small, the family expenses are huge, and the ownership of his father's estate is controlled by his stepmother, who cannot advise the small family. The income cannot cover the expenses, resulting in a high debt. Recently, the rent has also been in arrears for several months. The debtors are pressing from all sides, and he has no way to cope. Therefore, he thought of committing suicide. He left a suicide note at home this morning and handed over the keys to the line. He wandered alone on the roads, hesitating and undecided. Thinking that living would mean owing debts that are difficult to repay temporarily, and that dying would mean not being able to comfort his wife and children, he was caught in a dilemma. After thinking it over again and again, he finally decided to die. Therefore, he planned to commit suicide by jumping into the river. The head of the police verified the confession and ordered Detective Huang Songsheng to summon his wife. She took her husband home that night.

Wang Wenguang, a Ningbo native, 19 years old, with both parents alive, worked in the accounting room on the Anning ship. This year, the ship entered the dock for repairs, and Wang was also laid off. There are three relatives in Shanghai, one is his cousin Wang Lianfu, who works at the Xieji Bookstore on Datong Road, one is his sister Wang, who lives at No. 19, Taide Li, Xinzha, and one is his maternal uncle, who is the old manager at the Yuhua Xiang Machine Shop at No. 488, Oujia Road. Wang also stayed at these three places from time to time. However, being unemployed for a long time, he inevitably felt economically strained. Feeling that he was very uninteresting, he developed a world-weary thought. At around 2 PM yesterday, he took a small ferry from Yongxing Foreign Bank at Nanjing Road Wharf to Pudong. Wang jumped into the water as soon as the ship reached the heart of the river, intending to end his life. The old man Quanlin immediately stopped the ship and rescued him. When asked why he committed suicide, he simply cried. He was sent to the water patrol police station and questioned. Detective Huang Songsheng was dispatched to summon his cousin Wang Lianfu to the police station to take Wang away.

The Public Works Bureau Discusses the Issue of Building More Parks 163

The Public Works Bureau held a regular meeting of directors on Wednesday of this week. The acting accountant submitted a report suggesting that the matter of establishing more parks should be carried out after the Public Works Bureau has made a comprehensive plan for other important matters such as education and hospitals. Although the Public Works Bureau's special budget is expected to have a surplus by the end of this year, there are concerns that unexpected events may occur that require a large amount of money to cope with. The Director-General of the Public Works Bureau also said that a cautious approach should be taken. Although the sale of the electrical department can provide 30 million taels of silver to meet the needs, if about 8 million taels are used each year, the money will be exhausted in a few years, and the Public Works Bureau will be in a difficult situation again. The Board of Directors greatly praised the proposal for comprehensive financial planning. The Director-General stated that he also considered the construction of a park in the northern district to be an important task and that it could be started. A Director suggested that the Public Works Department should first make a detailed report on the area and the amount of money that could be obtained from the sale of the Public Works Bureau's surplus land, and then make a decision. At that time, the money from the sale of land could be used to purchase land for the construction of the park. Everyone then agreed with this proposal.

Imprisoned for Bigamy and Accused of Seeking Alimony 165

Wu Fuzhen Demands 7,200 Yuan

Wu Fuzhen, a woman from Suzhou, previously sued her husband Gao Jin, a gentry, for bigamy in the local court. It was alleged that she was introduced to Gao Jin as a second wife by a matchmaker on the tenth day of the tenth lunar month last year. Unexpectedly, after entering the door, she learned that the defendant's legal wife, Wu, was still in the home. The marriage location was at the China Hotel on Er Ma Road. The defendant denied the marriage, claiming that he paid 200 yuan to take the plaintiff as a concubine and did not formally marry her. The defendant's wife, Wu, also testified in court, saying that she could not have children due to illness, so she asked her husband to take a concubine for the sake of continuing the family line. After the court ordered the hotel waiter and the wedding equipment store owner to testify in court, it was proven that there was indeed a marriage ceremony. Therefore, Gao Jin was sentenced to three months' imprisonment for bigamy. The details have been reported in previous newspapers. It is now learned that Wu Fuzhen has hired lawyer Chen Wenzhao to petition the civil court for alimony for 20 years, totaling 7,200 yuan (calculated at 30 yuan per month), as well as clothing and other items worth 407 yuan. Judge Zhang Jinjian held a court hearing yesterday. He first telephoned the Caohejing Second Prison and sent the defendant Gao Jin to the court. According to the plaintiff Wu Fuzhen, she is a native of Suzhou, residing at No. 11, Anxiang Li, Datong Road, Zhabei, and provided a brief account of the previous situation, requesting alimony of 30 yuan per month. The official asked the defendant what business he was in and how much salary he earned each month. The defendant said that he was in the food business with a monthly salary of fifty to sixty yuan. The defendant Gao Jin stated that he was 30 years old, a native of Jiading, and worked as a partner in the Jushun Food Store on Douyi Street. He married Wu in 1927. Because she had a hidden illness, Wu suggested that he take a concubine, and he did not marry the plaintiff. The plaintiff now wants to leave me, but I have already paid 200 yuan. He does not want to leave. (Question) Who introduced her? (Answer) A man named Lu Genyi. They used deceptive means. (Question) Where does Lu live? (Answer) I don't know. (Question) The plaintiff is requesting 7,200 yuan in alimony. What do you think? (Answer) My salary in the food store is very low, only 16 yuan per month. Moreover, I have been in prison for several months, and I am afraid that the business will be hindered. Where will the alimony come from? I request a clear investigation. At this point, the plaintiff's lawyer said that if the alimony requested by the plaintiff is paid in one lump sum by the defendant, it will be 4,000 yuan. If it is paid in installments, it will be 30 yuan per month for 20 years. The interrogating officer believed that the debate was over and awaited the verdict. The defendant Gao Jin was ordered to be sent back to the Second Prison for confinement.

Disposition of Spring Medicine Cases 169

Six establishments, including the Zhongnan Pharmacy, were suspected of selling aphrodisiacs. The police requested a search warrant from the Special District Local Court and searched each establishment, finding various types of medicines in large quantities. However, the managers of these pharmacies failed to appear in court. The court ordered further summons for questioning. This matter was previously reported in this newspaper. It has now come to light that the Guangsi Jindan (Prolific Golden Pill) sold at the Bianxianglu (Fragrant Pavilion) in Pentang Lane also contains aphrodisiac ingredients. The police specially requested the court to summon its manager, who appeared yesterday morning. After questioning by Judge Xu, the court ordered a two-week adjournment and sent the presented medicine to the Shanghai Municipal Council Health Department for testing. Further interrogation will follow the report of the test results. The manager of the establishment was also instructed to send the Guangsi Jindan to the Central Testing Committee for legal testing. Furthermore, the case against Zhongnan and the other six pharmacies was ruled by Judge Shen of the Summary Court to be under the jurisdiction of the Local Court. The police then transferred the case to the First Criminal Court. After an individual interrogation by Judge Xu, the managers of the Aix and Zhongnan Pharmacies failed to appear for questioning. The court ordered arrest warrants. The medicines seized from the Geyan Congji She (Maxim Compilation Society) were sent to the Shanghai Municipal Council Health Department for testing. The society's representative, Yao Lianqing, was instructed to independently send the medicines sold to the Central Testing Committee for testing. A fourteen-day adjournment was granted, pending a report of the test results. Zhao Jicang, the principal of the Jicang Pharmaceutical Company, was fined fifteen yuan, and the medicines produced were confiscated. The products sold by the Zhongxi Department Store and the Bailing Company were found not to be aphrodisiacs, and their managers were declared innocent, with medicine ledgers returned.

A Lonely and Helpless Young Girl 170

Alone in the world, a bleak future

At around 9 PM the day before yesterday, a girl of about thirteen or fourteen years old was seen on Bailinan Road in Zhoujiaqiao, Shanghai West, wearing an old white calico shirt, black calico trousers, bare feet, and blue cloth shoes, wandering and crying miserably. A patrolling police officer noticed her and questioned her. Discovering that she was lost, the officer took her back to the 6th District Police Station. After questioning by District Chief Ren, the girl stated her name was Wu Guiying, thirteen years old, from Wuxi. She had come to Shanghai with her mother several years ago and worked in a Yangshupu cotton mill for seven months before returning home in the winter. Last year, her father suddenly died in mid-March, and her mother passed away in early October. She only has an older brother named Wenbing, twenty-two years old, who is not yet married. Because the family was very poor, they lacked the funds for coffins and burials and had to borrow from relatives to barely manage. Her brother had no job and wandered around at home, causing the siblings to live in dire straits. In March of this year, her brother suddenly left without saying goodbye. Neighbors, seeing her loneliness, took turns providing food to fill her stomach. A month later, her brother sent her a letter saying he had joined the army and gone north. Afterwards, she asked neighbors going to Shanghai if they would take her to Shanghai, saying she had an aunt (mother's sister) there and could find her and live with her. Because she was truly in distress, a neighbor agreed to bring her to Shanghai on the 29th of last month. They stayed overnight in a Yangshupu workshop, and the neighbor woman gave her four small silver coins to hire a rickshaw to Zhoujiaqiao to find her aunt. Unfortunately, the houses there had already been demolished and moved long ago. Having spent all her money and not knowing the way, she got lost. Recalling that her aunt (surnamed Wu) was nowhere to be found and her livelihood was cut off, she burst into tears. When asked for the neighbor's surname, she said she didn't know, only that they lived in the Yihe workshop in Yangshupu. District Chief Ren, feeling sorry for the girl's plight, decided to temporarily keep her at the station while they tried to find her aunt to claim her.

At around 10 AM the day before yesterday, the merchant ship Jin Yongxing was sailing from Shanghai to Wusong. Near Yingangpu, a small boat suddenly approached, flying the water police flag. The boat was carrying several police officers in uniform with rifles on their shoulders. One of the officers fired two shots into the air to stop the Jin Yongxing. The officers boarded the ship and rummaged through boxes, searching at will. The crew, seeing this situation, knew that these were pirates posing as water police to rob them. Fortunately, the ship was empty and had no cash on board, so the pirates were very dissatisfied. While they were coercing the crew, a fresh fish boat arrived. The pirates abandoned the Jin Yongxing to rob the fish boat. After escaping danger, the Jin Yongxing sailed to Wusong and reported to the Penglai Guild of Shipowners. Maintaining Civilian Food Supplies, Orders from the Hall 176

The Shanghai County Government yesterday received an order from the Jiangsu Civil Affairs Hall stating, "Regarding compliance with orders: A previous order from the Ministry of Interior stated that, concerning the issue of civilian food supplies, the Ministry has repeatedly issued orders to the civil affairs halls of various provinces to prohibit the export of rice and flour and to report on a timely basis for verification. Now, the difficulty of civilian food supplies has reached its extreme. The reason for this is both the result of poor harvests and the manipulation and raising of grain prices by unscrupulous merchants, as well as various improper consumptions, which should be strictly investigated and prohibited to avoid food shortages. At the same time, it should be quickly ordered that the subordinates prepare funds to carry out price stabilization in order to address both aspects. In addition to sub-issuing, it is necessary to reiterate the previous order, urging the hall to quickly comply and order its subordinates to earnestly handle the matter and report on the compliance situation for verification. This order is of utmost importance." Upon receiving this, in addition to sub-issuing orders, it is necessary to issue an order to the county magistrate, urging him to quickly comply with the handling and order his subordinates to uniformly prohibit and report the compliance situation for review. This order is of utmost importance.

○ Corpse Re-examination Issue for Yang Chunshan: Re-examination Must Dissect the Corpse, Cousin has no Right to Request Rejection

The body should be embalmed as soon as possible. Counterfeit Golden Mouse Brand Seized 180

Qiao Sanzi, the owner of Renhe Paper Shop on Ningbo Road in the French Concession, recently sold counterfeit Golden Mouse brand cigarettes produced by Huacheng Tobacco Company for petty profit. The method was to roll inferior tobacco (with paper printed with a similar Golden Mouse trademark) and place it in a genuine Golden Mouse brand cardboard box for sale, so that buyers could not detect it. This despicable act of deception was discovered by the inspection department of Huacheng Tobacco Company, which immediately reported it to the company's legal counsel, Te Pike, who, together with police detectives, searched the store. Four boxes of counterfeit cigarettes were seized on the spot. The detectives immediately arrested the store owner, Qiao Sanzi, and sent him to the French Concession Court for trial.

Fire on North Henan Road Yesterday 186

At 1:45 PM yesterday, a fire suddenly broke out in the kitchen of No. 665 North Henan Road. The fire quickly spread to the left and right to Nos. 664, 663, and 662. Fortunately, the fire brigade arrived and made every effort to put out the fire. After half an hour, the fire was extinguished. Lost Shaoxing Boy Awaiting Claim 187

The Municipal Public Security Bureau yesterday received a lost boy, Qin Chengfu, from the Fourth District. He claimed to be eleven years old, from Shaoxing. His ancestral home is in Yangjia, Shaoxing City. His mother works as a maid at the Yuyuanxiang store near the Ximen Xieqiao Bridge and fostered him at the Wang Qin tailor shop in Chen Fengtai. An investigation revealed that there was no Yuyuanxiang store near the Xieqiao Bridge, and it was impossible to find the child's mother for identification. He is now sent to the Xinpuyu Hall for custody awaiting claim.
